If you're not using an exact pattern with exact measures, this application will be very useful. \r\nIn the past 3 years, I've created over 50 quilts. Along the way, I learned a few time saving techniques and relearned some geometry. I've also repeated a few calculations on every quilt, such as the number of fabric strips for each quilt's bindings. I've shrunk quilt dimensions to save fabric and/or to provide a quilt for a twin bed instead of a king.\r\nI've loaded this application with calculations I either regularly make or I never want to manually make again (Square Hypotenuse and Square & Triangle Calculators).  I'm researching more calculators that will be available in updates. If you have a need for another calculator, please let me know.\r\nThis first update includes a new calculator and the addition of 3 Pattern helper calculators.","ProductFamilyName":"Apps","Schema":"Card;1"}],"Title":"Populære kjøpte","HasThirdPartyIAPs":false,"AlgoName":"RECO-Algo-Version","AlgoValue":"Lists;topPaid;;Apps;00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000003","TotalItems":974,"PageSize":200}}
